Fortunately, the housekeeper also asked him to help deal with it. The hotel is original and it is understandable that there are bugs. Later, four bugs were killed in the room within half an hour. Another one flew to the beam. The room was very high and I couldn‚Äôt hit it myself. I asked for help from the housekeeper. The aunt in the housekeeping depar**ent was enthusiastic and sincere. She popularized knowledge to us that the bug was a stink bug. Due to weather reasons, stink bugs were rampant. The hotel also arranged pest control and told us the correct way to deal with bugs. Finally, I changed the room and killed two more stink bugs in the new room. It was within the acceptable range and ended.
The hotel basically has no service except the aunt in the housekeeping depar**ent. I didn‚Äôt feel the service of a star hotel in the restaurant, swimming pool, afternoon tea bar, sports activity center and front desk, let alone smiling service. Every time I took the initiative to greet the hotel staff, it can be said that there was no basic courtesy. For example, when I contacted the guest service center by phone, the person who answered the phone was: "Hello, front desk." Even if I contacted the front desk in the company, at least they would say hello. I accepted these problems with an inclusive attitude. The presence of insects is a good sign for the ecology, and the hotel has also tried to kill them, so we should understand. I cannot be impolite when others are impolite, so we should be tolerant. The gym is about ten square meters, with a total of two treadmills, one of which cannot be used, and the other one's button control will fail during use, so just make do with it. The hotel gives people the feeling that as long as the supporting facilities are there, it's fine, as for whether they are good, can be used, and whether they are maintained, it's none of my business. I am also responsible for the hotel I choose. 
My emotional outburst point was when I contacted the guest service center for more bottled water, and the reply I got was that two bottles of water were provided free of charge a day, and the extra bottles were charged ten yuan each. It is understandable that the hotel formulates policies, and it is recommended to inform in advance on the hotel policy details page in the future, such as only providing two bottles of bottled water for free every day. For example, due to the original ecology of the hotel, it is normal for the total number of various insects in each room to be ‚â§ two. It is convenient for consumers to consider whether they can understand and accept it. 
I personally suggest that all kinds of hotel staff learn from the aunt in the housekeeping depar**ent about their service attitude and work attitude. Putting aside professionalism, what kind of work can be done if even the minimum work attitude is not correct? The enthusiasm and sincerity of the housekeeping auntie can be felt. She helps to find ways to catch insects, helps to get things when changing rooms, greets children warmly and proactively, cleans the room very cleanly, and delivers things very promptly. The hotel's service is so bad when the occupancy rate is not high. It's time to make some improvements. Blindly reducing labor costs will only lead to a vicious cycle and lower the overall quality of the hotel.
The last two points are based on the Chinese and Western food produced by the housekeeping auntie and the restaurant, which are affordable and taste good.
